id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_body" class="ajax__tab_body ajax__scroll_vert"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="visibility: visible;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures_ProductFeatureDesc"><h2><font style="color: #000000;">MARLIN</font></h2> <h2><font style="color: #000000;"><span>Model 1895SBL Large Loop .45-70 Government With 18.5 Inch Stainless Steel Barrel Laminated Stock XS Ghost Ring Sight System and XS Rail 5 Rounds</span></font></h2> <h2><font style="color: #000000;"><span>Big Loop lever action with heavy 18.5 inch stainless steel barrel, stainless steel receiver, trigger guard plate, loading gate and loop. Full length tubular magazine. Weather-impervious laminated stock. Features the XS Ghost Right Sight System and comes standard with a XS lever rail.</span></font></h2> <p><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3">Destined to be a top choice of North Country guides, it delivers the massive punch of a 45–70 Gov´t. with unmatched speed – with the lethal assurance of a 6–round capacity thanks to a full–length magazine tube. Rapid target acquisition comes natural with its 18½" barrel and XS Ghost Ring Sights and scout scope mount. And its big loop lever adds a distinctive traditional style while promoting sure follow-up shots, even with gloves. True to the inhospitable territory it was born to thrive in, the Model 1895SBL features the weather resistance of a grey/black laminated stock and stainless steel finish on all major metal components.</font></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/marlin/marlin_1895sbl.jpg" alt="" width="666" height="188"></p> <p><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3">The Marlin 1895SBL rifle has garnered quite a following. The latest accolade for this full-featured lever-action comes from OnTarget magazine. In the August 2009 issue, the editorial staff at OnTarget deemed the 1895SBL worthy of their 2009 Editor's Choice Award.&nbsp;</font><br><br><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3">Bill Battles, Editor of OnTarget, gives the Model 1895SBL high marks for its many innovative features saying, "With the XS® scout scope mount and aperture rear sight, the 1895SBL is ideally suited for fast-paced, close-quarters hunting."&nbsp;</font><br><br><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3">Chambered for the legendary 45-70 Government, the Model 1895SBL is built to handle the worst Mother Nature can throw its way. All major components - barrel, receiver, trigger guard plate, magazine tube, loading gate and enlarged loop lever; are constructed of durable stainless steel and housed in a weather-impervious black and gray laminated stock. Other distinctive features include 18 ½-inch heavy barrel contour, full length tubular magazine with 6-shot capacity, deluxe recoil pad and nickel-plated swivel studs.&nbsp;</font><br><br><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3">Ready for a quick call to action, the Model 1895SBL features the durable XS Ghost Ring Sight System which allows for faster target acquisition and improved accuracy over conventional sights. For those who prefer using optics, the 1895SBL comes standard with a XS Lever Scout Mount™ that provides a rock-solid mounting platform for a variety of options including long-eye relief scout scopes, traditional scopes and even red dot or holographic sights.&nbsp;</font><br><br><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3">Built for maximum performance and recognized by the editors of OnTarget magazine, the Model 1895SBL should be your rifle of choice.&nbsp;</font></p></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications_ProductsSpecifications"><ul><li>Category : Rifles</li><li>Action : Lever</li><li>Caliber : 45-70 Government</li><li>Barrel Length : 18.0"</li><li>Capacity : 5+1</li><li>Trigger : Standard</li><li>Safety : Hammer</li><li>OAL : 37"</li><li>Weight : 8 lbs</li><li>Stock Description : Laminate Gray</li><li>Metal Finish : Stainless Steel</li></ul></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Reviews"> <div id="Review"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_UpdatePnlProductReviewDetails"> <div class="Sorting"> <span class="TitleStyle"> Reviewed by <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_CustomersCnt">2</span> customer </span>&nbsp; <span> <select name="ctl00$ctl00$MainContent$uxProduct$uxProductTabs$ProductTabs$pnlCustomerReviews$uxProductReviews$RateList" onchange="javascript:setTimeout('__doPostBack(\'ctl00$ctl00$MainContent$uxProduct$uxProductTabs$ProductTabs$pnlCustomerReviews$uxProductReviews$RateList\',\'\')', 0)" id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_RateList" class="SortByDropdown"> <option selected="selected" value="desc">Newest First</option> <option value="asc">Oldest First</option> <option value="5">Highest Rating First</option> <option value="1">Lowest Rating First</option> </select> </span> </div> <div> <table id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_ReviewList" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;"> <tbody><tr> <td class="ReviewItem"> <div class="ItemStyle"> <div class="Title"> <span class="Subject"> awesome gun</span>, February 21, 2016</div> <div class="Content"> <div class="StarRating"> <img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/ShadeStar.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"></div> <div class="Row"> the only reason I didn't give it 5 stars is because it had some sharp edges from machining that I had to smooth out after I brought it home. I completely disassembled it, smoothed and polished the action, and it is as smooth as silk. all seems were tight between metal and wood and the front sight is at 12 o'clock as it should be. for me the ghost ring seems too big and is like looking at an ant through a stove pipe. i will eventually put a smaller diameter ghost ring on it.</div> <div class="Row"> By <span class="Text"> greenmoose</span> from <span class="Text"> nc</span></div> </div> </div> </td> </tr><tr> <td class="ReviewItem"> <div class="ItemStyle"> <div class="Title"> <span class="Subject"> Awesome rifle destined for legendary status</span>, January 10, 2015</div> <div class="Content"> <div class="StarRating"> <img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"></div> <div class="Row"> I can't say enough good things about this rifle. The balance and all the ergonomics are perfect. The oversized lever loop shows that someone built this "for use". Since most large game hunting is in Winter it stands to reason most people will be wearing gloves, right? The XS rail is perfect for mounting optics a little farther away than most rifles to prevent getting a black eye and the ghost ring sight with white front ramp sight are actually usable. The recoil pad really does it job. You'll be very glad its there and reduces recoil below 12ga shotgun levels. Stainless = less rusting than bluing. The laminate stock is beautiful and very rigid. I drilled some holes to mount an Accu-riser cheek pad and it was very hard to drill into. While most poo-poo the rainbow trajectory of the 45-70, the fact remains that with the proper load this round can drop anything with legs on every continent on Earth. Any seasoned hunter will tell you most shots are under 150yrds. Rounds range from 300gr to just under 600gr. Buy a rangefinder! This is my only rifle, but not my first. Be wary of the man with only one gun, for he surely knows how to use it. If you're even considering this rifle, buy it. You will never sell it.</div> <div class="Row"> By <span class="Text"> Daniel</span> from <span class="Text"> JBLM, Washington</span></div> </div> </div> </td> </tr> </tbody></table> </div> <div class="Paging"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_topNavigation"> <a id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_TopPrevLink" disabled="disabled">« Previous</a> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_lblPagingInfo"> | PAGE1 of 1 | </span> <a id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_TopNextLink" disabled="disabled">Next »</a> </div> </div> <div class="Spacer"> &nbsp;</div> <div> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_lblErrorMsg"></span></div> <div class="Spacer"> &nbsp;</div> </div> </div> </div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlAdditionalInformation" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="ShippingInfo"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlAdditionalInformation_ProductAdditionalInformation">This firearm ships to your local gun dealer/gun store (FFL dealer).
